Owing to the non-Markovian and non-semimartingale nature of the model, classical stochastic control techniques are not directly applicable. Instead, the problem is tackled using the martingale optimality principle by constructing a family of supermartingale processes characterized via solutions to an original Riccati backward stochastic differential equation with jumps (Riccati BSDEJ).The resulting optimal strategies for Merton's problems are derived in semi-closed form depending on the solutions to time-dependent multivariate Riccati-Volterra equations, while the optimal value is expressed using the solution to this original Riccati BSDEJ. Numerical experiments on a two-dimensional rough Heston model illustrate the impact of both path roughness and jumps components on the value function and optimal strategies in the Merton problem.

</details>


### [187] [A Line-search-free Method for Adaptive Decentralized Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00711)
*Xiaokai Chen,Ilya Kuruzov,Gesualdo Scutari*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种完全去中心化的自适应步长优化算法，每个智能体仅利用局部历史梯度和迭代点信息调整步长，无需全局调参或线搜索，并基于新构建的Lyapunov函数证明了凸和强凸情形下的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去中心化优化方法要么需要全局问题与网络参数的先验知识来调步长（不实用），要么需要昂贵的每迭代线搜索（需访问局部函数值）。本文旨在设计无需线搜索、无需全局调参、完全自适应的去中心化算法。

Method: 提出一种新的Lyapunov函数，从中自然导出自适应步长规则：每个智能体在每次迭代中，基于连续梯度构建局部曲率估计，选择保证下降的最大步长。算法仅利用过去局部迭代点和梯度，无需额外函数评估。

Result: 凸目标下证明次线性收敛率，强凸目标下证明线性收敛率。在标准基准测试上的数值实验一致优于现有自适应和非自适应最先进方法。

Conclusion: 本文证明了去中心化优化中可以实现完全自适应的步长选择，且不牺牲理论收敛保证，为实际部署提供了更实用的方案。

Abstract: We study decentralized optimization over networks where agents cooperatively minimize a smooth (strongly) convex sum of local losses while communicating only with immediate neighbors. Prevailing decentralized methods require either centralized knowledge of global problem and network parameters for stepsize tuning--hence impractical, or costly per-iteration line-searches that demand access to local function values. We propose line-search-free, fully decentralized algorithms in which each agent adapts its stepsize using only past local iterates and gradients--with no extra function evaluations and no global tuning. The key technical ingredient is a new Lyapunov function, from which a natural adaptive stepsize rule emerges: at each iteration, each agent selects the largest stepsize that guarantees descent, based solely on a local curvature estimate built from successive gradients. The proposed algorithms enjoy strong theoretical guarantees: sublinear convergence rates for merely convex objectives and linear rates under strong convexity. Numerical experiments on standard benchmarks show consistent improvements over the state of the art, both adaptive and non-adaptive.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展经典BLP模型，解决其未充分处理的市场份额持久性和内生性问题，提高需求估计的准确性。

Method: 在BLP框架中加入交互固定效应（因子结构）以捕捉未观测特征的共同因素，采用两步LS-MD（最小二乘-最小距离）程序进行估计。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟显示估计量表现良好，美国汽车需求实证分析验证了模型的有效性。

Abstract: We extend the Berry, Levinsohn and Pakes (BLP, 1995) random coefficients discrete-choice demand model, which underlies much recent empirical work in IO. We add interactive fixed effects in the form of a factor structure on the unobserved product characteristics. The interactive fixed effects can be arbitrarily correlated with the observed product characteristics (including price), which accommodates endogeneity and, at the same time, captures strong persistence in market shares across products and markets. We propose a two-step least squares-minimum distance (LS-MD) procedure to calculate the estimator. Our estimator is easy to compute, and Monte Carlo simulations show that it performs well. We consider an empirical illustration to US automobile demand.

### [189] [Dynamic Linear Panel Regression Models with Interactive Fixed Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00612)
*Hyungsik Roger Moon,Martin Weidner*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有交互固定效应和预定解释变量（如滞后因变量）的线性面板回归模型。在大N和大T渐近框架下，发现最小二乘估计量存在两种渐近偏差来源，并提出了偏差校正的LS估计量及三种经典检验统计量的偏差校正版本。蒙特卡洛模拟验证了有限样本下的良好表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论主要针对严格外生解释变量，而实际应用中常出现预定解释变量（如动态面板），导致LS估计量存在渐近偏差，需要完善其渐近理论并开发偏差校正方法。

Method: 在大N和大T联合渐近框架下，推导LS估计量的渐近分布，识别出两种偏差来源：一是 idiosyncratic误差项的相关性/异方差性，二是预定解释变量而非严格外生变量。在此基础上构造偏差校正的LS估计量，并推导Wald、LR和LM检验的偏差校正版本及其渐近卡方分布。通过蒙特卡洛模拟验证有限样本表现。

Result: 成功推导了LS估计量的渐近偏差来源，提出了偏差校正的LS估计量，并给出了三个经典检验的偏差校正版本，证明了其渐近服从卡方分布。蒙特卡洛模拟表明校正方法在有限样本中表现良好。

Conclusion: 本文为具有交互固定效应和预定解释变量的面板模型提供了完整的渐近推断理论，偏差校正方法有效改进了有限样本下的估计和检验表现。

Abstract: We analyze linear panel regression models with interactive fixed effects and predetermined regressors, for example lagged-dependent variables. The first-order asymptotic theory of the least squares (LS) estimator of the regression coefficients is worked out in the limit where both the cross-sectional dimension and the number of time periods become large. We find two sources of asymptotic bias of the LS estimator: bias due to correlation or heteroscedasticity of the idiosyncratic error term, and bias due to predetermined (as opposed to strictly exogenous) regressors. We provide a bias-corrected LS estimator. We also present bias-corrected versions of the three classical test statistics (Wald, LR, and LM test) and show their asymptotic distribution is a chi-squared distribution. Monte Carlo simulations show the bias correction of the LS estimator and of the test statistics also work well for finite sample sizes.

</details>


### [190] [Linear Regression for Panel With Unknown Number of Factors as Interactive Fixed Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00614)
*Hyungsik Roger Moon,Martin Weidner*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文研究了线性面板回归模型中存在未知数量交互固定效应时，最小二乘估计量的渐近性质。主要发现：只要估计时使用的因子数量不低于真实值，LS估计量的极限分布与使用的因子数量无关，因此无需一致估计交互固定效应的数量即可进行回归系数的统计推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在面板数据模型中，交互固定效应（因子结构）的存在使得回归系数的估计和推断变得复杂。传统方法需要先准确估计因子数量，但这一过程本身存在误差，可能导致后续推断不可靠。本文旨在探索是否能在不精确知道因子数量的情况下，仍然对回归系数进行有效的统计推断。

Method: 考虑线性面板回归模型，假设数据中存在未知数量的交互固定效应（因子）。在估计中使用的因子数量大于真实因子数量的条件下，推导当时间维度(T)和截面维度(N)联合趋于无穷时，回归系数LS估计量的极限分布。

Result: 建立了在过度设定因子数量（即估计时使用的因子数大于真实值）情况下，LS估计量的极限分布理论。关键发现：只要不过低估计因子数量，极限分布与所使用的因子数量无关。

Conclusion: 重要的实践意义：对回归系数进行推断时，不需要一致估计交互固定效应的数量。这简化了面板数据模型中的推断流程，降低了因因子数量误设带来的推断风险。

Abstract: In this paper we study the least squares (LS) estimator in a linear panel regression model with unknown number of factors appearing as interactive fixed effects. Assuming that the number of factors used in estimation is larger than the true number of factors in the data, we establish the limiting distribution of the LS estimator for the regression coefficients as the number of time periods and the number of cross-sectional units jointly go to infinity. The main result of the paper is that under certain assumptions the limiting distribution of the LS estimator is independent of the number of factors used in the estimation, as long as this number is not underestimated. The important practical implication of this result is that for inference on the regression coefficients one does not necessarily need to estimate the number of interactive fixed effects consistently.

</details>


### [191] [Penalized Likelihood for Dyadic Network Formation Models with Degree Heterogeneity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00771)
*Zizhong Yan,Jingrong Li,Yi Zhang*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种惩罚似然方法，同时解决网络形成模型中固定效应MLE存在性问题和 incidental-parameter 偏差问题，允许固定效应以对数速率发散，适用于稀疏大规模网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实证网络中，存在度异质性时有两个问题：(1) 零发链接、零收链接或链接所有人的代理会导致固定效应MLE不存在，而剔除这些代理会引入选择偏差；(2)  incidental-parameter问题会偏误公共参数和平均部分效应。

Method: 提出惩罚似然方法，主要规范模型为有向网络模型（含互惠性），嵌套了标准的无向和非互惠有向模型。惩罚项保证有限样本存在性，并对系数和部分效应进行偏差修正。渐近分析不要求固定效应紧致，允许其以对数速率发散。

Result: 该方法避免了选择偏差，恢复了稳健的参数估计，而传统方法在同样情况下失效。全球贸易应用验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的惩罚似然方法能够同时解决固定效应MLE的存在性问题和 incidental-parameter偏差，且适用于大规模稀疏网络，具有较强的实用价值。

Abstract: Estimating network formation models with degree heterogeneity raises two problems in empirical networks. First, agents that send no links, receive no links, or link to all remaining agents can make the fixed-effects MLE fail to exist. Trimming these agents changes the estimation sample and induces selection bias. Second, the incidental-parameter problem biases common parameters and average partial effects. We resolve both issues through a penalized likelihood approach. Our leading specification is a directed network model with reciprocity, nesting the standard undirected and non-reciprocal directed models. The penalty guarantees finite-sample existence and yields bias corrections for coefficients and partial effects. We establish asymptotic results without imposing compactness on the fixed-effects. Allowing the fixed effects to diverge at a logarithmic rate, our asymptotic framework accommodates the degree sparsity ubiquitous in large empirical networks. A global trade application demonstrates that our estimator avoids selection bias and recovers robust parameters where conventional methods fail.

</details>

### [192] [Distributed Observer Design for Discrete-Time LTI Systems via Jordan Canonical Form](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00210)
*Giulio Fattore,Maria Elena Valcher,Rui Gao,Guang-Hong Yang*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文针对离散时间线性时不变系统，基于Gao & Yang (2025)的框架，利用Jordan标准形提出两种分布式状态估计方案。方案一使用全维Luenberger观测器但需满足大量不等式；方案二条件更宽松但观测器阶数更高。两种方法均推导了保证渐近收敛的充要条件，且相比前人工作更灵活。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决分布式系统中各节点无法直接观测全局状态的问题，在Gao & Yang (2025)的基础上，寻求更灵活、约束更少的分布式状态估计方案。

Method: 利用系统矩阵的Jordan标准形，将状态分解为各节点局部可检测和不可检测两部分；对可检测部分使用Luenberger观测器，对不可检测部分采用一致性机制估计。提出两种方案：方案一保持观测器维度等于状态向量维度但不等式约束多；方案二放宽条件但观测器阶数增加。

Result: 推导了以系统矩阵特征值和通信网络拉普拉斯矩阵子矩阵特征值表达的充要条件，保证了分布式观测器渐近收敛。相比Gao & Yang (2025)，耦合增益选择更灵活，可解条件更宽松。

Conclusion: 本文提出的两种分布式估计方案在收敛性保证和条件宽松程度上优于现有工作，为分布式状态估计提供了更实用的设计工具。

Abstract: This paper addresses the problem of distributed state estimation for discrete-time linear time-invariant systems. Building on the framework proposed in Gao & Yang (2025), we exploit the Jordan canonical form of the system matrix to develop two distributed estimation schemes that ensure asymptotic convergence of local estimates to the true system state. In both approaches, each node reconstructs the components of the state that are locally detectable for it via a Luenberger observer, while employing a consensus-based mechanism to estimate the components that are not directly detectable.
  The first scheme relies on local observers whose dimension matches that of the original state vector; however, its applicability requires the satisfaction of a large set of inequalities. The second scheme, in contrast, can be implemented under less restrictive conditions, but results in observers of increased (augmented) order. For both methods, we derive necessary and sufficient conditions - expressed in terms of the eigenvalues of the system matrix and certain submatrices of the communication network Laplacian - that guarantee the existence of a distributed observer achieving asymptotically accurate estimation. Compared to Gao & Yang (2025), the proposed approaches offer greater flexibility in the selection of coupling gains and impose less stringent solvability conditions.

Applied to Hydro-Québec's projected 2035/2036 grid, the framework reveals critical insights under high wind and electric vehicle penetration. It also integrates an energy storage control strategy designed to mitigate wind variability and support grid reliability. Furthermore, AQSTSS facilitates the assessment of system resilience under diverse scenarios, including extreme weather and load variability. Motivation: AI数据中心电力负荷具有突发性和非平稳性，准确预测对实时运营效率和电网协调至关重要。现有高容量模型部署困难，而轻量级模型难以捕捉短时动态，存在精度与部署效率之间的权衡。

Method: 提出部署高效的知识蒸馏框架：(1) 训练高容量序列教师模型进行多步负荷轨迹预测，使用残差学习提升非平稳条件下的鲁棒性；(2) 开发轻量级点式学生模型，采用紧凑神经网络实现低延迟滚动推理；(3) 提出序列到点的蒸馏策略，通过对齐近端预测行为和时序池化表示来迁移时序知识。

Result: 在MIT Supercloud数据集上的案例研究表明，所提出的学生模型在预测精度上优于近期深度学习基线方法，同时将参数内存和模型规模的部署开销降低了10倍以上。

Conclusion: 该框架有效解决了AI数据中心负荷预测中精度与部署效率的权衡问题，通过知识蒸馏实现了高精度轻量级预测模型，具有实际部署价值。

Abstract: Accurately forecasting the bursty and non-stationary power demand of AI data centers has become increasingly important, as abrupt workload-driven variations at the GPU-node level can affect real-time operational efficiency, power management, and grid-data center coordination. However, high-capacity forecasting models are often difficult to deploy at scale because of their memory and latency requirements, while lightweight predictors may fail to capture short-horizon temporal dynamics. To address this accuracy-deployment tradeoff, this paper proposes a deployment-efficient knowledge distillation framework for short-term load forecasting in AI data centers. The proposed framework first trains a high-capacity sequence teacher model for multi-step load trajectory prediction, where residual learning is used to improve robustness under non-stationary operating conditions. A lightweight point-wise student model is then developed for low-latency rolling inference using a compact neural network architecture. To transfer temporal knowledge from the teacher to the student, a sequence-to-point distillation strategy is introduced by aligning near-term predictive behavior and temporally pooled representations. Case studies on the MIT Supercloud dataset demonstrate that the proposed student model improves forecasting accuracy over recent deep learning baselines while reducing the deployment footprint by over 10x in parameter memory and model size.

</details>


### [197] [The Potential Welfare Gains from Curtailment Trading Under Non-Firm Interconnection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00690)
*Richard Mahuze,Charlotte Gressel,Ali Amadeh,K. Max Zhang*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种网络约束的断电信用市场（CCM），通过双边信用流机制优化配电网中断负荷分配，相比按比例断电能提升1.24-1.83倍的总供电价值，并证明了其与理想中央规划器的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据中心等大负载快速增长导致电网容量紧张，而现有非刚性互联协议下的断电规则是"一刀切"式的，未考虑不同用户对断电损失（VOLL）的差异，造成经济效率低下。

Method: 提出网络约束的断电信用市场（CCM），代理提交反映真实中断成本的投标，形成受输电网络约束的双边信用流；将问题建模为双层优化，并转化为可精确求解的单层混合整数线性规划（MILP）。

Result: 在3节点玩具网络、IEEE 24节点测试系统和缩减的纽约电网三个系统上验证：CCM相比按比例断电提升总供电价值1.24-1.83倍；在激励兼容基准支付下，无参与者利益受损；MILP求解时间为0.01-83秒。

Conclusion: CCM机制在不损失分配能力的前提下（可行性集等价），通过市场化手段实现了比行政化按比例断电更优的负荷分配，兼顾效率与公平。

Abstract: Rapid growth of large loads led by data centers is straining grid capacity. These loads increasingly accept curtailment risk through non-firm interconnection agreements to gain faster grid access, expanding the pool of consumers subject to mandatory disconnection during supply shortfalls. Yet, blunt rules assign curtailment without reference to the wide variation in the value consumers place on avoiding curtailment, often captured by the value of lost load (VOLL). This paper introduces the network-constrained Curtailment Credit Market (CCM), a mechanism in which agents submit bids that determine bilateral credit flows, subject to transmission network constraints. We prove that the bilateral credit flow representation can reach every curtailment allocation available to an omniscient central planner (feasible-set equivalence), so the bilateral flow structure introduces no loss of allocative capability. Under truthful bidding, the CCM achieves the planner's total value of served load, matching the planner's allocative benchmark when bids reflect true interruption costs. The CCM is formulated as a bilevel clearing problem that admits an exact single-level mixed-integer linear program (MILP), solved in 0.01 to 83 seconds. Numerical experiments on three test systems validate the mechanism at increasing scale and complexity: a 3-bus toy network that isolates the core trading logic, the IEEE 24-bus reliability test system as a standard benchmark, and a reduced New York (NY) grid that captures coordination across NY load zones. Our simulations show that the CCM increases the total value of served load by 1.24 to 1.83 times relative to pro-rata curtailment. On the three test systems examined here, no participant is worse off under incentive-compatible benchmark payments than under the administrative baseline.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 1) SSSC广泛部署在小中型容量线路上，减少需要加固的输电通道数量；2) 年化系统成本降低19亿美元；3) 输电扩展需求减少20%；4) 中西部地区部署的效益成本比高达59，有助于将中西部风电输送至东部负荷中心。

Abstract: Flexible AC Transmission Systems (FACTS), particularly Static Synchronous Series Compensators (SSSC), can improve network transfer capability and complement restricted transmission expansion. Evaluations of FACTS within large-scale, real-world power system planning are currently lacking. This paper develops a capacity expansion model for the contiguous U.S. power system toward 2050, incorporating SSSC-modified linear power flow equations and accounting for impedance feedback in transmission expansion. Cost-optimal system expansion leverages widespread nationwide SSSC deployment on small-to-medium capacity lines and reduces the number of corridors to be reinforced. Overall, SSSCs reduce annualized system costs by $1.9 billion or decrease transmission expansion requirements by 20%. The most advantageous deployments achieving benefit-cost ratios of 59 concentrated in the Midwest, facilitating the delivery of central U.S. wind power to eastern load centers. The value proposition of SSSCs is robust to cost sensitivities and potential competition from HVDC network expansion, and increases under higher demand growth and more stringent decarbonization policies. These findings provide a blueprint for leveraging SSSC deployment in the U.S. power system.

### [200] [Voltage Ride-Through in Large Loads- A Dual PQ Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00769)
*Amir Norouzi,Michael Morel*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型负载（如AI数据中心）的电压穿越问题，指出传统无功补偿方法因容量和电网约束存在局限，提出了一种新的有功与无功（PQ）联合控制方法，并分析了极端电压跌落时负载可能不得不脱离电网的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型负载（如AI数据中心）在电网暂态扰动期间的电压穿越能力对电力系统稳定性和可靠性至关重要，而传统无功补偿方法在容量和电网约束下效果有限，因此需要探索更有效的电压穿越方案。

Method: 首先对大型负载的电压穿越问题进行数学分析，揭示传统无功补偿方法的局限性；然后提出一种双有功-无功（PQ）联合控制方法，利用具有动态P和Q调节能力的非电网资源辅助电压穿越；最后通过实际数值算例验证分析结果。

Result: 传统无功补偿方法因配电基础设施容量和电网约束存在极限，无法充分保证大型负载的电压穿越；提出的PQ联合方法需要非电网资源的动态有功和无功支持；在极端电压跌落条件下，维持可接受的负载电压可能不可行，导致负载脱网。

Conclusion: 大型负载电压穿越不能仅依赖无功补偿，需要引入具有动态有功和无功调节能力的非电网资源；极端工况下负载脱网可能是不可避免的结果。

Abstract: This paper provides a detailed investigation of voltage ride-through in large loads, such as Artificial Intelligence data centers. Voltage ride-through capability of large loads during transient disturbances in the power grid is important because of the potential impact on the stability and reliability of the Bulk Power System. A mathematical analysis is presented and it is shown how the traditional approach, based on reactive power compensation, may not be adequate for voltage ride-through in large loads. Ultimately, due to capacity limits of the load's power distribution infrastructure and grid's constraints, there is a limit to using reactive power as a corrective tool. A new dual active and reactive power (PQ) approach is proposed in which non-grid resources with dynamic P and Q capabilities are shown to be needed to help with voltage ride-through. Additionally, the analysis illustrates that at extreme voltage dips in the power grid maintaining an acceptable level of load voltage can become practically or theoretically unattainable, which may lead to the load's disconnection from the grid. Analytical results are provided with practical numerical examples.

Abstract: As climate extreme and disaster events become more frequent and intense, Geospatial Artificial Intelligence (GeoAI) has emerged as a transformative approach for large-scale disaster mapping and risk reduction. However, the purely mechanical, performance-driven deployment of GeoAI models can result in amplifying inherent spatial inequalities, preventing effective emergency decision-making, and producing severe environmental carbon footprint. To unbox the concept of responsible GeoAI, this position paper examines its emerging role, e.g., in climate extreme and disaster mapping, from a critical GIS perspective. We address the nexus of responsible GeoAI into four interrelated theoretical dimensions, specifically Representativeness, Explainability, Sustainability, and Ethics, with examples from climate extreme and disaster mapping. Moreover, targeting at the operational practice, we then propose a conceptual governance Model of responsible GeoAI that categorizes its governance practices into Data, Application, and Society scopes. ### [202] [AI Adoption Among Teachers: Insights on Concerns, Support, Confidence, and Attitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00343)
*Vanessa B. Sibug,Maria Anna D. Cruz,Vicky P. Vital,Juvy C. Grume,Almer B. Gamboa,Emerson Q. Fernando,Lloyd D. Feliciano,Jordan L. Salenga,John Paul P. Miranda*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了制度支持、教师信心和教师担忧在AI教育工具采纳中的作用。通过对260名菲律宾教师的调查发现，制度支持显著预测教师信心和态度，但教师担忧不调节这一关系；信心完全中介了制度支持对态度的正向影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI在教育领域的广泛应用，理解影响教师采纳AI工具的因素至关重要。已有研究关注制度支持和教师个体因素，但教师担忧作为调节变量的作用尚不明确，研究旨在揭示三者之间的内在机制。

Method: 对260名菲律宾教师进行问卷调查，计算制度支持、信心、担忧和态度的复合分数；采用有调节的多重回归分析检验调节效应，并进一步进行中介分析（Sobel检验）检验信心的中介作用。

Result: 制度支持显著正向预测教师信心和态度；教师担忧未显著调节这些关系；信心完全中介了制度支持对态度的影响，间接效应显著（Sobel检验），直接效应在加入信心后不显著。

Conclusion: 制度支持通过增强教师信心来改善其对AI的态度，而非通过缓解担忧。建议教育机构提供结构化、持续的支持（如专业发展、导师指导），将AI融入教师教育项目，以提升教师准备度和AI采纳效果。

Abstract: The study examines the adoption of artificial intelligence (AI) tools in education by analyzing the roles of institutional support, teacher confidence, and teacher concerns. It aims to determine whether teacher concerns moderate the relationship between institutional support and two outcomes: teacher confidence and attitudes toward AI adoption. The sample included 260 teachers from the Philippines. Composite scores were calculated for institutional support, confidence, concerns, and attitudes. Moderated multiple regression analysis showed that institutional support significantly predicted both teacher confidence and attitudes toward AI. However, teacher concerns did not significantly moderate these relationships. A follow-up mediation analysis tested whether confidence explains the effect of institutional support on attitudes. Results showed full mediation. The indirect effect was significant based on the Sobel test, and the direct effect became non-significant when confidence was included in the model. This shows that institutional support improves teacher attitudes by increasing their confidence. The study recommends that institutions provide structured and ongoing support to strengthen teacher confidence. Professional development, mentoring, and AI integration in teacher education programs can increase readiness and support effective AI adoption.

This chapter applies text mining to publications indexed in a leading academic database to map scholarly discourse on ChatGPT in programming education. Term frequency analysis, phrase pattern extraction, and topic modeling reveal four dominant themes: pedagogical implementation, student-centered learning and engagement, AI infrastructure and human-AI collaboration, and assessment, prompting, and model evaluation. The literature prioritizes classroom practice and learner interaction, with comparatively limited attention to assessment design and institutional governance. These findings support responsible integration and highlight the need for stronger assessment and governance mechanisms.

### [204] [Adaptive Norm-Based Regularization for Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00171)
*Muhammad Qasim,Farrukh Javed*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了两种针对神经网络的正则化方法：一种是将输入特征协方差结构融入岭回归型ℓ2惩罚的协方差感知权重衰减，另一种是结合ℓ1稀疏惩罚与协方差感知ℓ2惩罚的混合正则化。通过蒙特卡洛模拟和两个真实数据实验（建筑冷负荷预测、白血病基因表达分类），证明该方法在特征相关或高维场景下优于标准正则化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络范数正则化方法（如标准权重衰减）未考虑输入特征之间的依赖关系，在特征相关或高维场景下复杂度控制效果有限，需要设计能利用特征协方差信息的正则化策略。

Method: 提出两种正则化策略：1) 协方差感知的岭型ℓ2惩罚，将输入特征协方差结构融入权重衰减；2) 结合ℓ1稀疏惩罚与协方差感知ℓ2惩罚的混合正则化，产生既稀疏又受结构信息约束的神经网络权重。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟和两个真实数据实验（建筑冷负荷预测、白血病高维基因表达分类）表明，所提出的正则化方法在未见数据上的预测性能优于标准范数惩罚，尤其在特征相关或高维场景下复杂度控制更有效。

Conclusion: 将特征协方差结构融入神经网络正则化可以有效提升模型在特征相关和高维场景下的泛化性能，为神经网络的正则化设计提供了新的结构感知方向。

Abstract: In this paper, we study norm-based regularization methods for neural networks. We compare existing penalization approaches and introduce two regularization strategies that extend classical ridge- and lasso-type penalties to neural network models. The first strategy modifies weight decay by incorporating the covariance structure of the input features into a ridge-type $\ell_2$ penalty, allowing regularization to account for feature dependence. The second combines an $\ell_1$ sparsity penalty with covariance-aware $\ell_2$ regularization, producing neural network weights that are both sparse and structurally informed. Monte Carlo simulations are used to evaluate these methods under different data-generating settings, followed by two real-data applications on building cooling-load prediction and leukemia cell-type classification from high-dimensional gene expression data. Across simulated and real-data examples, the proposed regularizers improve predictive performance on unseen data and provide more effective complexity control than standard norm-based penalties, particularly when features are correlated or high-dimensional.

</details>


### [205] [SHIFT: Robust Double Machine Learning for Average Dose-Response Functions under Heavy-Tailed Contamination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00176)
*Eichi Uehara*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出SHIFT——一种结合Welsch损失、渐进非凸优化和防御性OLS重拟合的稳健双机器学习估计器，在污染场景下将水平RMSE从1.03降至0.33，并能高精度恢复异常值掩码，同时配套极值理论诊断工具集以指导方法选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统双机器学习中核加权局部线性平滑器对异常值敏感，单个异常值会偏置整个核窗口内的曲线估计，缺乏稳健性。

Method: SHIFT框架：交叉拟合干扰正交化 + 核局部Welsch损失的渐进非凸优化二阶估计 + 基于残差MAD而非原始结果MAD的防御性OLS重拟合。同时提供六种极值理论诊断方法（Hill、GPD-MLE/PWM、GEV、Mean Excess、参数稳定性、因果尾系数）来指导方法选择。

Result: 在p=0.25的局部污染测试中，水平RMSE从1.03降至0.33；1400次主扫描中，最坏情况形状恢复RMSE为0.325（仅次于Huber-DML的0.276）；异常值掩码恢复平均F1≈0.96。线性干扰模型在均匀污染下优于梯度提升模型。

Conclusion: SHIFT在稳健性、异常值检测能力方面表现优异，且附带的诊断工具集为实际应用提供了理论指导；反直觉发现：均匀污染下线性干扰模型更优，颠覆了"越灵活越好"的传统认知。

Abstract: Double-machine-learning pipelines for the Average Dose-Response Function rely on kernel-weighted local-linear smoothers, which inherit unbounded functional influence: a single outlier within a kernel window biases the curve across the entire window. We introduce SHIFT (Self-calibrated Heavy-tail Inlier-Fit with Tempering), a robust DML estimator combining cross-fit nuisance orthogonalization with a kernel-local Welsch-loss second stage optimized by Graduated Non-Convexity, and -- the principal design choice -- a defensive OLS refit whose inlier cutoff is scaled by post-GNC residual MAD rather than the raw-outcome MAD. On a localized-contamination stress test at $p=0.25$ this design choice drops level-RMSE from 1.03 to 0.33 while leaving clean and uniformly-contaminated runs unchanged. Across 1,400 main-sweep fits, SHIFT has competitive worst-case shape recovery (RMSE $0.325$ at $p=0.25$, second to Huber-DML's $0.276$); among the three methods with worst-case RMSE below $0.35$, only SHIFT emits a non-uniform per-sample weight vector, recovering the ground-truth outlier mask at mean $F_1 \approx 0.96$ (range $0.945$--$0.968$) on Gaussian-jump DGPs. We pair the estimator with a six-technique Extreme Value Theory diagnostic suite (Hill, GPD-MLE/PWM, GEV, Mean Excess, parameter stability, causal tail coefficient) that lets a practitioner distinguish Frechet from Weibull regimes and choose between SHIFT and L1 alternatives on empirical grounds. Extensions to binary-treatment CATE (Huber pseudo-outcome X-Learner) and time-series ADRF (block-CV + rolling MAD) are included. A counter-intuitive ablation: linear nuisance models (Ridge, Lasso) outperform gradient-boosted nuisances for robust DML under uniform contamination, inverting the usual more-flexible-is-better heuristic.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（伴随方法、分数匹配等）在指数倾斜目标分布采样问题中缺乏统一的理论框架，且不同方法在梯度方差、收敛性等方面存在差异，需要系统性的理论分析来指导方法选择与改进。

Method: 从随机最优控制视角统一框架，通过偏置-方差分解分析不同分数匹配方法的梯度方差性质，推导伴随ODE的范数界来理论支持伴随方法有效性，并将CMCD和NETS损失函数以及Crooks-Jarzynski恒等式适应到指数倾斜设置中。

Result: 发现Adjoint Matching/Sampling和Novel Score Matching具有有限梯度方差，而Target和Conditional Score Matching则不具有；证明了伴随方法的理论优势；提出了适应指数倾斜场景的新损失函数与热力学恒等式。

Conclusion: 通过Stable Diffusion的奖励微调实验验证了理论分析的正确性和方法的有效性，为指数倾斜分布采样提供了统一的理论框架和实践指导。

Abstract: We study the problem of training diffusion and flow generative models to sample from target distributions defined by an exponential tilting of a base density; a formulation that subsumes both sampling from unnormalized densities and reward fine-tuning of pre-trained models. This problem can be approached from a stochastic optimal control (SOC) perspective, using adjoint-based or score matching methods, or from a non-equilibrium thermodynamics perspective. We provide a unified framework encompassing these approaches and make three main contributions: (i) bias-variance decompositions revealing that Adjoint Matching/Sampling and Novel Score Matching have finite gradient variance, while Target and Conditional Score Matching do not; (ii) norm bounds on the lean adjoint ODE that theoretically support the effectiveness of adjoint-based methods; and (iii) adaptations of the CMCD and NETS loss functions, along with novel Crooks and Jarzynski identities, to the exponential tilting setting. We validate our analysis with reward fine-tuning experiments on Stable Diffusion 1.5 and 3.

### [207] [Information-geometric adaptive sampling for graph diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00250)
*Yuhui Lu,Wenjing Liu,Kun Zhan*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于信息几何的图生成扩散采样框架，通过Fisher-Rao度量定义漂移变分分数（DVS），实现了等弧长采样策略，在分子和社交网络生成任务上显著提升了结构保真度和采样效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准图生成扩散模型使用均匀时间步长，忽略了复杂流形上分布演化的非均匀动态特性，需要更合理的几何感知采样策略。

Method: 将扩散采样轨迹重新解释为黎曼流形上的参数曲线，利用Fisher-Rao度量分析内在距离，推导出漂移变分分数（DVS）作为几何感知指标，并设计等信息速度求解器实现均匀分布变化率的采样。

Result: 在分子和社交网络生成任务上，DVS方法在结构保真度和采样效率方面均显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 基于信息几何的等弧长采样策略能有效提升图生成扩散模型的性能，DVS为采样动力学提供了Fisher-Rao意义下的局部刚性刻画。

Abstract: Standard diffusion models for graph generation typically rely on uniform time-stepping, an approach that overlooks the non-homogeneous dynamics of distributional evolution on complex manifolds. In this paper, we present an information-geometric framework that reinterprets the diffusion sampling trajectory as a parametric curve on a Riemannian manifold. Our key observation is that the Fisher-Rao metric provides a principled measure of the intrinsic distance. By analyzing this metric, we derive the Drift Variation Score (DVS), a geometry-aware indicator that quantifies the instantaneous rate of distributional change. Unlike prior heuristic-based adaptive samplers, our DVS solver enforces a constant informational speed on the statistical manifold, automatically maintaining a uniform rate of distributional change along the sampling trajectory. This equal arc-length strategy ensures that each discretization step contributes equally to the information speed. Theoretical analysis verifies that DVS characterizes the local stiffness of the sampling dynamics in the Fisher-Rao sense. Experimental results on molecule and social network generation show that DVS significantly improves structural fidelity and sampling efficiency. Code is at https://github.com/kunzhan/DVS

### [208] [Gradient Regularized Newton Boosting Trees with Global Convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00581)
*Nikita Zozoulenko,Daniel Falkowski,Thomas Cass,Lukas Gonon*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了受限牛顿下降（Restricted Newton Descent）框架，统一了牛顿提升（Newton Boosting）与经典有限维理论。证明了标准牛顿提升在光滑强凸损失下的线性收敛率，并针对一般凸损失提出自适应ℓ2正则化方案，达到O(1/k²)收敛率，匹配带Nesterov动量的一阶提升方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 牛顿提升（如XGBoost、LightGBM、CatBoost）在经验上表现优异，但其全局收敛性理论上远不如一阶提升方法清晰，缺乏系统性理解。

Method: 1）提出Restricted Newton Descent框架，基于余弦角和弱梯度边缘概念，在Hilbert空间中研究牛顿法的不精确迭代优化。2）针对光滑强凸损失证明线性收敛率。3）针对一般凸损失（Lipschitz Hessian），引入自适应ℓ2正则化项（正比于梯度范数平方根），修改经典算法得到全局收敛的O(1/k²)速率。

Result: 1）标准牛顿提升在Hessian主导条件下线性收敛。2）提出的正则化牛顿提升方案取得O(1/k²)全局收敛率，匹配一阶Nesterov加速方法。3）数值实验表明新方案收敛，而标准牛顿提升可能发散。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上填补了牛顿提升全局收敛性的空白，提出的自适应正则化方案兼具理论保证与实用效果，为二阶GBDT算法提供了坚实的收敛性基础。

Abstract: Gradient Boosting Decision Trees (GBDTs) dominate tabular machine learning, with modern implementations like XGBoost, LightGBM, and CatBoost being based on Newton boosting: a second-order descent step in the space of decision trees. Despite its empirical success, the global convergence of Newton boosting is poorly understood compared to first-order boosting. In this paper, we introduce Restricted Newton Descent, which studies convex optimization with Newton's method on Hilbert spaces with inexact iterates, based on the concepts of cosine angle and weak gradient edge. Within this framework, we recover Newton boosting with GBDTs and classical finite-dimensional theory as special cases. We first prove that vanilla Newton boosting achieves a linear rate of convergence for smooth, strongly convex losses that satisfy a Hessian-dominance condition. To handle general convex losses with Lipschitz Hessians, we extend a recent gradient regularized Newton scheme to the restricted weak learner setting. This scheme minimally modifies the classical algorithm by introducing an adaptive $\ell_2$-regularization term proportional to the square root of the gradient norm at each iteration. We establish a $\mathcal{O}(\frac{1}{k^2})$ rate for this scheme, thereby obtaining a globally convergent second-order GBDT algorithm with a rate matching that of first-order boosting with Nesterov momentum. In numerical experiments, we show that our scheme converges while vanilla Newton boosting may diverge.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统贝叶斯设计和计算机化自适应测试依赖严格的参数假设或昂贵的后验近似，难以处理异质性高维数据和冷启动场景。作者希望通过引入人格诱导的潜在变量模型来解决这些局限性。

Method: 提出人格诱导潜在变量模型，将用户状态建模为有限AI人格字典的成员隶属度。每种人格由大语言模型生成响应分布。利用有限混合模型实现闭式后验更新和高效预测，从而在顺序项目选择中实现可扩展的贝叶斯设计。

Result: 在合成数据和WorldValuesBench数据集上的实验表明，基于人格的后验分布能够提供准确的概率预测，并构建可解释的自适应询问流程。

Conclusion: 该方法在保持计算高效性的同时，克服了传统方法的参数假设限制，为高维、异质性和冷启动场景下的自适应询问提供了可行且可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: We study adaptive querying for learning user-dependent quantities of interest, such as responses to held-out items and psychometric indicators, within tight question budgets. Classical Bayesian design and computerized adaptive testing typically rely on restrictive parametric assumptions or expensive posterior approximations, limiting their use in heterogeneous, high-dimensional, and cold-start settings. We introduce a persona-induced latent variable model that represents a user's state through membership in a finite dictionary of AI personas, each offering response distributions produced by a large language model. This yields expressive priors with closed-form posterior updates and efficient finite-mixture predictions, enabling scalable Bayesian design for sequential item selection. Experiments on synthetic data and WorldValuesBench demonstrate that persona-based posteriors deliver accurate probabilistic predictions and an interpretable adaptive elicitation pipeline.

### [210] [Decentralized Proximal Stochastic Gradient Langevin Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00723)
*Mohammad Rafiqul Islam,Lingjiong Zhu*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出了一种去中心化近端随机梯度朗之万动力学（DE-PSGLD）算法，用于在凸约束域上进行对数凹概率分布的采样。通过Moreau-Yosida包络实现约束处理，并给出了2-Wasserstein距离下的非渐近收敛保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的去中心化MCMC方法无法处理有约束的采样问题，而实际应用中许多后验分布都定义在有界或凸约束域上。作者希望填补这一空白，提出首个适用于约束域的去中心化采样算法。

Method: 基于Moreau-Yosida包络的共享近端正则化技术，将约束优化转化为无约束更新问题；结合去中心化随机梯度朗之万动力学（SGLD）框架，在分布式节点间进行信息交互与采样。

Result: 建立了单个智能体迭代及其网络平均在2-Wasserstein距离下的非渐近收敛界；量化了近端近似引入的偏差；在合成和真实数据集上的实验验证了快速后验集中性和高预测精度。

Conclusion: DE-PSGLD是首个针对约束域的去中心化MCMC方法，理论分析与实验均表明其在约束域采样任务中具有良好性能，为分布式贝叶斯推断提供了新思路。

Abstract: We propose Decentralized Proximal Stochastic Gradient Langevin Dynamics (DE-PSGLD), a decentralized Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) algorithm for sampling from a log-concave probability distribution constrained to a convex domain. Constraints are enforced through a shared proximal regularization based on the Moreau-Yosida envelope, enabling unconstrained updates while preserving consistency with the target constrained posterior. We establish non-asymptotic convergence guarantees in the 2-Wasserstein distance for both individual agent iterates and their network averages. Our analysis shows that DE-PSGLD converges to a regularized Gibbs distribution and quantifies the bias introduced by the proximal approximation. We evaluate DE-PSGLD for different sampling problems on synthetic and real datasets. As the first decentralized approach for constrained domains, our algorithm exhibits fast posterior concentration and high predictive accuracy.

</details>
